import requests

URL = 'https://www.google.com/search?pz=1&cf=all&ned=us&hl=en&tbm=nws&gl=us&as_q={query}&as_occt=any&as_drrb=b&as_mindate={month}%2F%{from_day}%2F{year}&as_maxdate={month}%2F{to_day}%2F{year}&tbs=cdr%3A1%2Ccd_min%3A3%2F1%2F13%2Ccd_max%3A3%2F2%2F13&authuser=0'

responses = []
def run(**params):
    response = requests.get(URL.format(**params))
    print(response.content, response.status_code)
    responses.append(response.content)

import pandas as pd
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
table = ''
soup = BeautifulSoup(responses[0], 'lxml') # Parse the HTML as a string
    
table = soup.find_all('a')[25:] # Grab the first table
row_marker = 0
tables = []
tables2 = []
final = {}
for i in range(len(table)-19):
    row = table[i]
    column_marker = 0
    columns = row
    if (columns):
        tables.append(columns.get_text())
        tables2.append(columns['href'])
for i in range(len(tables)):
    final[i] = {'href': tables2[i],'text': tables[i]}

final2 = pd.DataFrame(final)
final2 = final2.T
